<Text>I don't normally give "5 Star" reviews because I seldom think that anything is "perfect", BUT I had a perfect experience with Milo yesterday.  I was thinking of buying some snowboards for my two boys Amazon or some other mass merchandiser, but a friend told me to call Milo before I made any decisions.  I was helped by Brady at Milo and the experience was great.  He is extremely knowledgeable and excellent with customer service.  Brady answered all of my questions - that would've never been answered on other sites.  I ended up buying (2) snowboard packages with confidence that I got exactly the right boards and the best price.  And, they told me to bring the boards back for a free waxing.  I shipped to (2) different locations with no hassles and they even wrote a "happy birthday" note for one of the shipments.  Later, I received a follow up call from Brady.  Excellent customer service, excellent board shop.  The whole experience re-shaped how I am going to buy all products in the future - more local, "real" shops and less of the bland amazon experience. < Text>
Baileys Cove state park is hard for me to rate on the single 5 star system.
As a small 7 space camping park with a attached day use area. Its really nice!
The current (3-13-2021) camp host, Brian had the park looking good. No trash to be seen and the bathrooms were clean.
I would have to give a small deduction for being located under a portion of 1-5. So naturally, you do hear some heavy truck traffic while around the camp fire / picnic area. This may bother some light sleepers or those in tents.
At only $25 a night (3-13-21). It's a great place to camp for someone traveling 1-5...

The negative is that unfortunately, Baileys Cove as a WATER recreation area is impossible. The fact of the matter is, do to a variety of reasons. The Cove is bone DRY in mid March. My attached photos can far better put it into perspective, then my words...
With NO snow pack to speak of when I visited / went by the Mt. Shasta area. I don't see or know now Mt. Shasta lake can refill up enough water, to once again restore Bailey's Cove as a water recreation area any time soon. Pretty sad...<//Text>

Lance G<//user_name>
< date>
1532659345506<//date>
< Rate>
3< /Rate>
< text>
Came here to camp for one night in late July. While this campground is right by Shasta Lake, there really isn't much water to speak of this time of the year. Mind you, it is deep enough to swim in, but dont expect a very ample lake in Summer.

The campgrounds themselves are quite nice - nicely laid out, and many of them feel quite private and spacious. The very first one does offer a bit of a lake view, although you'll be right by the entrance and, as I mentioned, there isn't that much of a lake. Do note that you are fairly close to the highway, but the noise isn't overly loud.

Come night time, there are bugs galore - putting aside the mosquitoes, there are swarms of these tiny little bugs that aren't warded off by citranella candles, and there was this one class of beetle that literally would dive bomb my table in a dazed and drunken state - entertaining, but annoying.

Finally, in July in more or less central California, it's hot as heck, so expect that.

However, I'm being a little petty - it was a nice campground, and I'd probably recommend this place in the early springtime when the water levels would be higher and temperatures lower. Cost when I went was $20 per night. There is drinking water, but you have to bring your own firewood.< /text>

We decided to try this place out since they had a family meal deal. $25 for 4 burgers and 2 orders of fries. My family is big, so we ordered chicken strips for the little ones. < review>
The large pretzel starter is great with any of the cold local beers on tap. It's good with the entire variety of course,  but supporting local brewers makes it taste better. Steins available too for quenching your thirst.  Ordered the bison burger, one of the best I've ever had.  When bingo started, the host passed out cards and blotters to the people who were interested in playing, mostly reservations. Believe it or not,   I won the first 2 bingo games of the night! My prizes were a free beer on my next visit, which I'm sure will be another memorable experience. Great location next to the old Vogue theatre, featuring  a variety of outdoor seating. Family friendly.  There's clearly a reason this place stays busy, and I look forward to my next visit.

Highly recommended.<//review>

Ike's has great sandwiches for all tastes and dietary requirements. I usually don't go for fake meat, but this place has some great options. They have a variety of meat, vegetarian and vegan options with multiple bread choices. Their dutch crunch is my favorite. Sandwiches are quite big and very filling.
